<U>Messages<UC><C><L.36.1>
<L.6.1>
<Z>Slack <C> There's a independent (i.e. I'm not on it) group on Slack of various players in various games (Gameplan, Raceplan, <L.31.1>
Baseball, Run Chase and Dark Age - but other channels are welcome) covering things run here. For more information, go to <L.31.1>
gameplanpbm.slack.com, or for an invite people can contact Alan Milnes at alan@gameplan.org.uk.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Early Warning <C> I should be away on holiday from 11th to 18th September, so we'll have some of the usual late running of<L.31.1>
turns when that happens (unhelpfully, both the Premier League and NFL kickoff that weekend). I'll provide more details closer<L.31.1>
to the time of how turns will be affected.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Free Startups <C> I'm still running the offer of a free startup (first two turns) in any of the games currently running.<L.31.1>
The rationale is simple, it's straightforward for me to do, there's a fair chance some folk out there might be looking to pick <L.31.1>
up an old game, and yes, somewhere down the line you may have to pay for the turns, though that's far from the driving force. <L.31.1>
If you fancy taking up a new team, or reviving your existing one, drop me an email. Feel free to flag up these games to <L.31.1>
friends and family - the more the merrier when people have time on their hands.<L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Late Turns <C> Deadlines are 9am Saturday. Please assume weekend turns will be run either Saturday or Sunday (i.e. please<L.31.1>
don't chase me up Sunday for "missing turns"). I run these games in my spare time, so the more efficient that is the better. <L.31.1>
<L.12.1>
<Z>Playing Online/Postage Costs <C> Note that from the start of April, I'm now considering all games to be "online first", and<L.31.1>
if you do want/need a posted copy of the results, there's an extra 0.4 credit charge. Please try and use email if possible<L.31.1>
